<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-manifest_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-manifest-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       was the penultimate mission of\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n        NASA\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_program" title="Space Shuttle program">\n        Space Shuttle program\n       </a>\n       and the 25th and last spaceflight of\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n         Space Shuttle\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This flight delivered the\n       <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer" title="Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer\n       </a>\n       and an\n       <a href="/wiki/ExPRESS_Logistics_Carrier" title="ExPRESS Logistics Carrier">\n        ExPRESS Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sched_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sched-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       served as the mission commander. STS-134 was expected to be the final space shuttle mission if\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">\n        STS-135\n       </a>\n       did not receive funding from\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">\n        Congress\n       </a>\n       . However, in February 2011, NASA stated that STS-135 would fly "regardless" of the funding situation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       STS-135, flown by\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , took advantage of the processing for STS-335, the\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        Launch On Need\n       </a>\n       mission that would have been necessary if the STS-134 crew became stranded in orbit.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Changes in the design of the main payload, AMS-02, as well as delays to\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-133" title="STS-133">\n        STS-133\n       </a>\n       , led to delays in the mission. The first launch attempt on 29 April 2011 was scrubbed at 12:20\xc2\xa0pm by launch managers due to problems with two heaters on one of the orbiter\'s auxiliary power units (APU).\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       launched successfully at 08:56:28 EDT (12:56:28 UTC)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       on 16 May 2011,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and landed for the final time on 1 June 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-edition.cnn.com_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-edition.cnn.com-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n   <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a Feustel">\n          Andrew J. Feustel\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         Second spaceflight\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Mission Specialist 4\n        </th>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <span class="flagicon">\n          <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n           <img alt="United States" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>\n          </a>\n         </span>\n         <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Chamitoff" title="Gregory Chamitoff">\n          Gregory Chamitoff\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         Second spaceflight\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="3">\n         <b>\n          Notes:\n         </b>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           On 13 January 2011, after the\n           <a href="/wiki/2011_Tucson_shooting" title="2011 Tucson shooting">\n            2011 Tucson shooting\n           </a>\n           in which Congresswoman Gabrielle Giffords, Mark Kelly\'s wife, was critically wounded, NASA named\n           <a href="/wiki/Frederick_W._Sturckow" title="Frederick W. Sturckow">\n            Frederick W. Sturckow\n           </a>\n           as backup commander for this mission.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n            <a href="#cite_note-20">\n             [20]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Roberto Vittori from Italy was the last non-U.S. astronaut to fly with the shuttle.\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Background">\n        Background\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Background">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_4" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:854px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_5" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/37/STS-134_launch_2.ogv/STS-134_launch_2.ogv.160p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Low bandwidth src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/37/STS-134_launch_2.ogv/STS-134_launch_2.ogv.240p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Small WebM (240P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 240P" data-transcodekey="240p.webm" data-width="426" data-height="240" data-bandwidth="316104" data-framerate="25"/&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/37/STS-134_launch_2.ogv/STS-134_launch_2.ogv.360p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="WebM (360P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 360P" data-transcodekey="360p.webm" data-width="640" data-height="360" data-bandwidth="577744" data-framerate="25"/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\'>\n         <img alt="File:STS-134 launch 2.ogv" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/STS-134_launch_2.ogv/220px--STS-134_launch_2.ogv.jpg" style="width:220px;height:124px"/>\n         <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/STS-134_launch_2.ogv" target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_launch_2.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         STS-134\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n          Space Shuttle\n         </a>\n         launch\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_program" title="Space Shuttle program">\n        Space Shuttle\n       </a>\n       had been scheduled to be retired from service after\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-133" title="STS-133">\n        STS-133\n       </a>\n       , but controversy over the cancellation of several\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       components, most notably the\n       <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer" title="Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer\n       </a>\n       , in order to meet deadlines for the retirement of the shuttle, caused the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Government" title="United States Government">\n        United States Government\n       </a>\n       to consider ordering an additional mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approve_21-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-approve-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On 19 June 2008, the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">\n        United States House of Representatives\n       </a>\n       passed the NASA Authorization Act of 2008, giving\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n        NASA\n       </a>\n       funding for one additional mission to "deliver science experiments to the station".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approve_21-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-approve-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The same mandate was included in the U.S. Senate version of the NASA Authorization Act that was unanimously approved by the Senate Committee on Commerce, Science, and Transportation on 25 June 2008.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-loc_22-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-loc-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was amended and passed by the full Senate on 25 September 2008, passed by the House on 27 September 2008, and signed by President\n       <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">\n        George W. Bush\n       </a>\n       on 15 October 2008.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HR6063_23-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HR6063-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-act2_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-act2-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Bush had previously opposed any additional shuttle missions, as they could delay the transition to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Project_Constellation" title="Project Constellation">\n        Project Constellation\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nc_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nc-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the spring of 2009, the Obama Administration included funds for the STS-134 mission in its proposed 2010 NASA budget.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       STS-134 was planned to be the final regularly scheduled mission of the NASA Space Shuttle Program, but with the passing in 2011 of an appropriations bill authorizing the conversion of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/STS-335" title="STS-335">\n        STS-335\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-135" title="STS-135">\n        STS-135\n       </a>\n       , this was no longer the case.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was also originally scheduled to coincide with\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_26" title="Expedition 26">\n        Expedition 26\n       </a>\n       before delays in the Space Shuttle launch schedule pushed it past that Expedition. If STS-134 had launched during Expedition 26, then Mark Kelly and Expedition 26 commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Scott_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Scott Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Scott Kelly\n       </a>\n       would have become the first siblings (and twins) to fly in space at the same time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Shuttle Commander Mark Kelly\'s wife,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Representative" title="U.S. Representative">\n        U.S. Representative\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Giffords" title="Gabrielle Giffords">\n        Gabrielle Giffords\n       </a>\n       , flew to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       (KSC) in Florida to view the first launch attempt, her first trip since moving from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tucson" title="Tucson">\n        Tucson\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Houston" title="Houston">\n        Houston\n       </a>\n       for rehabilitation after being seriously wounded in the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Tucson_shooting" title="2011 Tucson shooting">\n        January 2011 Tucson shooting\n       </a>\n       . On 16 May, Giffords was again at KSC for the launch, which was "one of the most anticipated in years," according to\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">\n         The New York Times\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        U.S. President Barack Obama\n       </a>\n       scheduled a visit to Kennedy Space Center on 29 April 2011 to view the launch,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and despite the canceled launch attempt he toured an\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Processing_Facility" title="Orbiter Processing Facility">\n        Orbiter Processing Facility\n       </a>\n       at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Launch_Complex_39" title="Launch Complex 39">\n        Launch Complex 39\n       </a>\n       and met with Giffords and the six crewmembers.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_payload">\n        Mission payload\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Mission payload">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg/220px-STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg/330px-STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg/440px-STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_closeup_of_AMS-02_in_space_shuttle_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A close up view of\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMS-2" title="AMS-2">\n          AMS-2\n         </a>\n         inside\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n          \'\n         </span>\n         s payload bay shortly before it was installed on the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer_2">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer 2\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer 2">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer" title="Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer" title="Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer 2\n       </a>\n       (AMS-02) was carried to the ISS in\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s payload bay, and was attached to the ISS\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        S3 truss\n       </a>\n       segment. The AMS-02 unit is a particle physics detector which contains a large permanent\n       <a href="/wiki/Magnet" title="Magnet">\n        magnet\n       </a>\n       , and is designed to search for\n       <a href="/wiki/Antimatter" title="Antimatter">\n        antimatter\n       </a>\n       and investigate the origin and structure of\n       <a href="/wiki/Dark_matter" title="Dark matter">\n        dark matter\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       According to the original design plan, a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cryogenic" title="Cryogenic">\n        cryogenic\n       </a>\n       , superconducting magnet system was developed for the AMS-02. This was reported by NASA to be a critical technology, granting the instrument the high sensitivity needed to achieve mission objectives.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Late in its development, however, poorly understood anomalous heating in the cryogenic magnet system was discovered. As a result, the AMS-02 experiment leader,\n       <a href="/wiki/Samuel_C._C._Ting" title="Samuel C. C. Ting">\n        Samuel C. C. Ting\n       </a>\n       , decided to replace the superconducting magnet inside the spectrometer with the permanent magnet previously used in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMS-01" title="AMS-01">\n        AMS-01\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="ExPRESS_Logistics_Carrier_3">\n        ExPRESS Logistics Carrier 3\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: ExPRESS Logistics Carrier 3">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="469" data-file-width="887" height="116" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg/220px-ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg/330px-ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg/440px-ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ELC-3_STS-134_Launch_Config.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ELC-3" title="ELC-3">\n          ELC-3\n         </a>\n         in its launch configuration\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/ExPRESS_Logistics_Carrier" title="ExPRESS Logistics Carrier">\n        ExPRESS Logistics Carrier 3\n       </a>\n       (ELC3) carried several Orbital Replacement Units (ORU) that were too large or too heavy for other spacecraft to carry to the ISS. These ORUs included a High Pressure Gas Tank (HPGT), an Ammonia Tank Assembly (ATA), the\n       <a href="/wiki/S_band" title="S band">\n        S band\n       </a>\n       Antenna Sub-System Assembly #2 &amp; 3 (SASA), a\n       <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n        Special Purpose Dextrous Manipulator\n       </a>\n       (SPDM) Arm with Orbital Replacement Unit change-out mechanism, a Space Test Program Houston 3\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">\n        Department of Defense\n       </a>\n       payload, and a spare ELC pallet controller avionics box.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Materials_on_International_Space_Station_Experiment">\n        Materials on International Space Station Experiment\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Materials on International Space Station Experiment">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The STS-134 mission delivered the\n       <a href="/wiki/Materials_International_Space_Station_Experiment" title="Materials International Space Station Experiment">\n        Materials on International Space Station Experiment 8\n       </a>\n       (MISSE) experiments, and returned the completed MISSE 7 experiments to Earth. MISSE 7 had been delivered to the ISS on\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-129" title="STS-129">\n        STS-129\n       </a>\n       in 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sensor_Test_of_Orion_Rel-nav_Risk_Mitigation_Detailed_Test_Objective_kit">\n        Sensor Test of Orion Rel-nav Risk Mitigation Detailed Test Objective kit\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Sensor Test of Orion Rel-nav Risk Mitigation Detailed Test Objective kit">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The Orion Rel-nav Sensor was mounted on the Orbiter Docking System (ODS) in\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Trajectory_Control_Sensor&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Trajectory Control Sensor (page does not exist)">\n        Trajectory Control Sensor\n       </a>\n       slot 1 and on an Adaptive Payload Carrier in the bay 3 port of the Payload Bay. For the STORRM Detailed Test Objective (DTO), after\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       undocked, it completed its normal fly-around of the station. The crew then guided\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       back towards the station, flying a nominal orbiter trajectory for docking to the ISS\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Pressurized_Mating_Adapter" title="Pressurized Mating Adapter">\n        Pressurized Mating Adapter-2\n       </a>\n       . However, the shuttle did not actually dock with the ISS again; instead, it was positioned below the station.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-131" title="STS-131">\n        STS-131\n       </a>\n       , the docking target on the ISS was enhanced with reflectors, to allow for the characterization of the Orion Rel-Nav sensors\' performance during STS-134\'s rendezvous and proximity operations with the ISS. These proximity operations were tested during approach and docking, undocking, flyaround (time permitting), and during a modified separation from the ISS. During the modified separation, the crew performed a series of re-rendezvous burns that put the orbiter on an Orion-like rendezvous profile. Afterwards, instead of re-docking to the ISS, the crew performed a full separation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="GLACIER_Freezer_Module">\n        GLACIER Freezer Module\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: GLACIER Freezer Module">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       STS-134 carried a new\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GLACIER_(ISS_Facility)" title="GLACIER (ISS Facility)">\n        Glacier\n       </a>\n       module to the ISS and returned two old ones to Earth. The Glacier units were used to store and return science samples on the space shuttle.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg/220px-STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg/330px-STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg/440px-STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA4_the_Enhanced_International_Space_Station_Boom_Assembly.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The newly attached\n         <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n          OBSS\n         </a>\n         at the\n         <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n          Space Station\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       STS-134 left its\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) permanently on the ISS for use in reaching places that the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       cannot get to on its own.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-obss_2-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-obss-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The usefulness of having an OBSS available for use at the station was demonstrated during\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scott_Parazynski" title="Scott Parazynski">\n        Scott Parazynski\n       </a>\n       \'s repair of the torn P6 solar panel on\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-120" title="STS-120">\n        STS-120\n       </a>\n       . The feasibility of leaving an OBSS attached to ISS for a long period of time was demonstrated when the\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-123" title="STS-123">\n        STS-123\n       </a>\n       mission left one behind for use during the subsequent\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-124" title="STS-124">\n        STS-124\n       </a>\n       mission.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lego_kits">\n        Lego kits\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Lego kits">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       brought 13\n       <a href="/wiki/Lego" title="Lego">\n        Lego\n       </a>\n       kits to the ISS, where astronauts built Lego models to see how they would react in microgravity, as part of the\n       <i>\n        Lego Bricks in Space\n       </i>\n       program. The results were shared with schools as part of an educational project.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Banks_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Banks-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Eaton_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Eaton-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shuttle_LIFE">\n        Shuttle LIFE\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Shuttle LIFE">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Living_Interplanetary_Flight_Experiment" title="Living Interplanetary Flight Experiment">\n        LIFE\n       </a>\n       precursor mission was launched aboard Endeavour. This\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Planetary_Society" title="Planetary Society">\n        Planetary Society\n       </a>\n       project was to test the mission destined for\n       <a href="/wiki/Fobos-Grunt" title="Fobos-Grunt">\n        Fobos-Grunt\n       </a>\n       . The stage rehearsal was deemed fully successful.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="STEM_Bars">\n        STEM Bars\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: STEM Bars">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       brought specialized nutrition bars, called "STEM Bars", to the ISS. These were created by high school students and sisters Mikayla and Shannon Diesch. The nutrition bars were certified for spaceflight by meeting a specific NASA-developed nutritional profile, and had to pass strict microbial testing. The STEM Bars were flown to support the work of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Battle_Creek,_Michigan" title="Battle Creek, Michigan">\n        Battle Creek, Michigan\n       </a>\n       -based sisters to raise awareness of the importance of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/STEM_fields" title="STEM fields">\n        STEM education\n       </a>\n       among their peers, an outreach effort which they started after they won the 2010\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Conrad_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Conrad Foundation (page does not exist)">\n        Conrad Foundation\n       </a>\n       Spirit of Innovation Awards.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hien_38-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hien-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="The_Little_Mole">\n        The Little Mole\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: The Little Mole">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       A\n       <a href="/wiki/Figurine" title="Figurine">\n        figurine\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mole_(Zden%C4%9Bk_Miler_character)" title="Mole (Zden\xc4\x9bk Miler character)">\n        Little Mole\n       </a>\n       was successfully brought back to earth by\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Andrew_Feustel" title="Andrew Feustel">\n        Andrew Feustel\n       </a>\n       . It was later presented to the character\'s creator,\n       <a href="/wiki/Zden%C4%9Bk_Miler" title="Zden\xc4\x9bk Miler">\n        Zden\xc4\x9bk Miler\n       </a>\n       , and used for space science popularization mainly in the Czech Republic.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_experiments">\n        Mission experiments\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Mission experiments">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       performed four\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">\n        Department of Defense\n       </a>\n       payloads of opportunity: MAUI, SEITI, RAMBO-2, and SIMPLEX. All four of these experiments required engine and thruster firings, and were to be completed only if there was sufficient propellant on board\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_milestones">\n        Mission milestones\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Mission milestones">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The mission marked:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        165th NASA manned space flight\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        134th shuttle mission since\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-1" title="STS-1">\n         STS-1\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        25th flight of\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        36th shuttle mission to the ISS\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        109th post-\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Challenger" title="Space Shuttle Challenger">\n          Challenger\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        mission\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        21st post-\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia" title="Space Shuttle Columbia">\n          Columbia\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        mission\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Last non-US astronaut to fly on a Space Shuttle mission (Col.\n        <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Vittori" title="Roberto Vittori">\n         Roberto Vittori\n        </a>\n        , Italy)\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shuttle_processing">\n        Shuttle processing\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Shuttle processing">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rollout">\n        Rollout\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Rollout">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Rollout of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       commenced on 10 March 2011 at 19:56 EST and terminated on 11 March 2011 at 03:49 EST.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Endevour_Rollout_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Endevour_Rollout-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional     </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n     </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Shuttle_Endeavour_sitting_on_LC-39A_shortly_after_RSS_retract.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="3018" data-file-width="4527" height="80" Launch Pad 39A.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Launchpad_fatality">\n        Launchpad fatality\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Launchpad fatality">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       At around 07:40 EDT on 14 March 2011,\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Space_Alliance" title="United Space Alliance">\n        United Space Alliance\n       </a>\n       engineer James Vanover committed suicide\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       by jumping from the STS-134 launchpad.\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       was at the pad when the incident occurred. As a result, work on the space shuttle was suspended for the day while\n       <a href="/wiki/Grief_counseling" title="Grief counseling">\n        grief counseling\n       </a>\n       was offered to the workforce. NASA officials believed this to be the first launchpad fatality since 1981.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-myfoxorlando-1_43-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-myfoxorlando-1-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-itwire-1_44-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-itwire-1-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Mission timeline">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="16_May_(Flight_Day_1_\xe2\x80\x93_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="16_May_.28Flight_Day_1_.E2.80.93_Launch.29">\n        16 May (Flight Day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 16 May (Flight Day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_launch_12.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-134_launch_12.jpg/220px-STS-134_launch_12.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-134_launch_12.jpg/330px-STS-134_launch_12.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-134_launch_12.jpg/440px-STS-134_launch_12.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_launch_12.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n          Space Shuttle\n          <i>\n           Endeavour\n          </i>\n         </a>\n         launches from\n         <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n          Kennedy Space Center\n         </a>\n         on STS-134.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       lifted off from\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Launch_Complex_39" title="Launch Complex 39">\n        Launch Complex 39\n       </a>\n       at 08:56 EDT on 16 May 2011. The launch of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       came after an on-time tanking process which filled the shuttle\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_external_tank" title="Space Shuttle external tank">\n        external tank\n       </a>\n       with more than 1,900,000\xc2\xa0l (500,000 US gallons) of\n       <a href="/wiki/Liquid_oxygen" title="Liquid oxygen">\n        liquid oxygen\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Liquid_hydrogen" title="Liquid hydrogen">\n        liquid hydrogen\n       </a>\n       ; the tanking started at 23:36 EDT on 15 May 2011. Once the shuttle and crew were on-orbit, they set about preparing the shuttle for the mission ahead. The first tasks they completed were opening the payload bay doors, activating the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ku_band" title="Ku band">\n        K\n        <sub>\n         u\n        </sub>\n        -band\n       </a>\n       antenna, and activating the Shuttle Remote Manipulator System (SRMS), also known as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        Canadarm\n       </a>\n       . Prior to this, commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       and pilot\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       completed an engine firing, known as the OMS-2 burn, to circularize the orbit of the shuttle. They also completed another engine firing, the NC-1 burn, to help the shuttle catch up to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS). After completing these initial tasks, the crew activated the\n       <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Magnetic_Spectrometer" title="Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer">\n        Alpha Magnetic Spectrometer\n       </a>\n       , allowing it to be monitored by teams on the ground. Later in the crew\'s work day, they downlinked video recordings that had been shot of the external tank by mission specialist\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd01_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd01-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width:      </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           The launch of\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           seen from a shuttle training aircraft.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="17_May_(Flight_Day_2_\xe2\x80\x93_OBSS_inspection)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="17_May_.28Flight_Day_2_.E2.80.93_OBSS_inspection.29">\n        17 May (Flight Day 2 \xe2\x80\x93 OBSS inspection)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 17 May (Flight Day 2 \xe2\x80\x93 OBSS inspection)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg/220px-A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg/330px-A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg/440px-A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:A_delighted_Mike_Fincke_STS-134.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n          Mike Fincke\n         </a>\n         lifts heavy bags and floats freely inside\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 2, the crew of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       completed several tasks in preparation for the docking on flight day 3. The first and most important of these tasks was surveying the shuttle\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermal_Protection_System" title="Thermal Protection System">\n        Thermal Protection System\n       </a>\n       (TPS).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-foxfd2_46-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-foxfd2-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) was used to survey the wing leading edge and nose cone. The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shuttle_Remote_Manipulator_System" title="Shuttle Remote Manipulator System">\n        Shuttle Remote Manipulator System\n       </a>\n       (SRMS, or Canadarm 1) was also used to look at the thermal tiles and blankets on and around the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbital_Maneuvering_System" title="Orbital Maneuvering System">\n        Orbital Maneuvering System\n       </a>\n       (OMS) pods. After the survey was complete, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Express_Logistics_Carrier" title="Express Logistics Carrier">\n        Express Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       (ELC) 3 was grappled by the SRMS.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat3_47-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat3-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While the survey was conducted by Greg Johnson and mission specialists\n       <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Vittori" title="Roberto Vittori">\n        Roberto Vittori\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       , the rest of the crew prepared the orbiter for docking. This included installing tools such as a center-line camera in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbiter_Docking_System" title="Orbiter Docking System">\n        Orbiter Docking System\n       </a>\n       , along with various other sensors used to gauge distance and speed. Kelly and mission specialists\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n        Drew Feustel\n       </a>\n       furthermore checked out the two spacesuits carried on\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       , in preparation for the mission\'s four planned spacewalks.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="18_May_(Flight_Day_3_\xe2\x80\x93_ISS_rendezvous_and_ELC_installation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="18_May_.28Flight_Day_3_.E2.80.93_ISS_rendezvous_and_ELC_installation.29">\n        18 May (Flight Day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 ISS rendezvous and ELC installation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 18 May (Flight Day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 ISS rendezvous and ELC installation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg/220px-STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg/330px-STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg/440px-STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Endeavour_approaches_the_space_station.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         approaches the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n          space station\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 3 saw the docking of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pressurized_Mating_Adapter" title="Pressurized Mating Adapter">\n        Pressurized Mating Adapter\n       </a>\n       (PMA) 2 on the ISS. The docking occurred on 18 May 2011 at 10:14\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dock_48-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-dock-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After the shuttle docked, the six astronauts of STS-134 joined the\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       crew on board the ISS. The joint crews completed a series of leak checks and opened the hatches at 11:38 UTC. Once the hatches were open, the joint crew held a welcome ceremony and completed a safety briefing. The first task for the joint crew was to unberth the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Express_Logistics_Carrier" title="Express Logistics Carrier">\n        Express Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       (ELC) 3, and attach it to its final location on the ISS\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Port 3\n       </a>\n       (P3) truss segment. Express Logistics Carrier 3 was removed from the payload bay of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        SRMS\n       </a>\n       and handed off to the Space Station Remote Manipulator System (SSRMS), also known as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       . The ELC 3 was finally installed at 16:18 UTC. Kelly began to transfer oxygen from space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       to the ISS. Mike Fincke and Drew Feustel transferred the two\n       <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Mobility_Unit" title="Extravehicular Mobility Unit">\n        Extravehicular Mobility Units\n       </a>\n       (EMU) to the ISS\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quest_Airlock" title="Quest Airlock">\n        <i>\n         Quest\n        </i>\n        Airlock\n       </a>\n       in preparation for their use during the mission\'s four spacewalks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat5_49-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat5-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg/120px-STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg/180px-STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg/240px-STS-134_Endeavour%27s_payload_bay_and_partly_obscured_ISS.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           With an extended docking ring\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           approaches the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            ISS\n           </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg/120px-STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg/180px-STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg/240px-STS_134_Endeavour%27s_Close_Up.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n            \'\n           </span>\n           s starboard wing photographed by a\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            Station\n           </a>\n           crew member.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg/120px-Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg/180px-Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg/240px-Expedition_27_and_STS-134_crew_members_shortly_after_the_hatches_were_opened.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           STS-134 and\n           <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27"  <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_ELC-3_in_the_grasp_of_Endeavour%27s_robotic_arm.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80"        </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ELC-3" title="ELC-3">\n            ELC-3\n           </a>\n           in the grasp of\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n            \'\n           </span>\n           s robotic arm.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="19_May_(Flight_Day_4_\xe2\x80\x93_AMS-2_installation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="19_May_.28Flight_Day_4_.E2.80.93_AMS-2_installation.29">\n        19 May (Flight Day 4 \xe2\x80\x93 AMS-2 installation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 19 May (Flight Day 4 \xe2\x80\x93 AMS-2 installation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg/220px-STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg/330px-STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg/440px-STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_the_starboard_truss_of_the_ISS_with_the_newly-installed_AMS-02.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         Starboard truss with the newly installed\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMS-02" title="AMS-02">\n          AMS-02\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The STS-134 crew installed the AMS-2 on flight day 4. AMS-2 was lifted out of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s payload bay using the Canadarm, operated by Drew Feustel and Roberto Vittori. It was handed off to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       , which was operated by\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       , and was installed in its final location on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        S3 truss segment\n       </a>\n       at 09:46 UTC. Immediately after the installation, crews on the ground began activating the experiment. The installation of the AMS-2 marked the completion of the\n       <a href="/wiki/US_Orbital_Segment" title="US Orbital Segment">\n        US Orbital Segment\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-complete_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-complete-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later in the day, Greg Chamitoff, Drew Feustel and Mike Fincke prepared the\n       <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Mobility_Unit" title="Extravehicular Mobility Unit">\n        Extravehicular Mobility Units\n       </a>\n       (EMU) that Chamitoff and Feustel would wear during their spacewalk on flight day 5. The trio was also assisted by commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       in preparing the tools required for the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Activity" title="Extravehicular Activity">\n        Extravehicular Activity\n       </a>\n       (EVA). While this was going on,\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       crew members\n       <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Nespoli" title="Paolo Nespoli">\n        Paolo Nespoli\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cady_Coleman" title="Cady Coleman">\n        Cady Coleman\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n        Ron Garan\n       </a>\n       assisted the rest of the STS-134 crew in completing transfers to and from\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       . Late in the crew day, the two crews performed an EVA procedures review. After the review, Chamitoff and Feustel camped out in the\n       <i>\n        Quest\n       </i>\n       Airlock overnight, in preparation for the mission\'s first spacewalk. The campout was done with the airlock\'s air pressure reduced, so as to purge\n       <a href="/wiki/Nitrogen" title="Nitrogen">\n        nitrogen\n       </a>\n       bubbles from the astronauts\' blood and thus prevent\n       <a href="/wiki/Decompression_sickness" title="Decompression sickness">\n        decompression sickness\n       </a>\n       . Members of both crews also conducted two in-flight interviews with media on the ground, including\n       <a href="/wiki/PBS_NewsHour" title="PBS NewsHour">\n        PBS NewsHour\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Public_Radio" title="National Public Radio">\n        National Public Radio\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Associated_Press" title="Associated Press">\n        Associated Press\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">\n        Reuters\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fox_News" title="Fox News">\n        Fox News\n       </a>\n       . The crew also answered questions that were relayed up to them by\n       <a href="/wiki/Miles_O%27Brien_(journalist)" title="Miles O\'Brien (journalist)">\n        Miles O\'Brien\n       </a>\n       for\n       <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">\n        Google\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat7_51-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat7-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/120px-STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/180px-STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/240px-STS-134_view_from_the_Cupola_to_space_shuttle_Endeavour.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n            Dextre\n           </a>\n           in the center as\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            Station\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n            \'\n           </span>\n           s Canadarm2 transfers\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMS-02" title="AMS-02">\n            AMS-02\n           </a>\n           for installation.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS_134_Endeavour_Docked_At_The_ISS.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="4288" data-file-width="2844" </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           docked at the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            ISS\n           </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Roberto_Vittori_floats_through_the_Destiny_lab.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80"      </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Vittori" title="Roberto Vittori">\n            Roberto Vittori\n           </a>\n           floats through the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Destiny_laboratory" title="Destiny laboratory">\n            Destiny laboratory\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="20_May_(Flight_Day_5_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="20_May_.28Flight_Day_5_.E2.80.93_EVA_1.29">\n        20 May (Flight Day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 20 May (Flight Day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The first spacewalk of the STS-134 mission was completed on flight day 5.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n        Drew Feustel\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       completed the installation of a new set of\n       <a href="/wiki/Materials_International_Space_Station_Experiment" title="Materials International Space Station Experiment">\n        MISSE experiments\n       </a>\n       , and also started installing a new wireless video system, but were stopped when a CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       sensor failed in Chamitoff\'s suit. After the failure, the pair were told to install an\n       <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">\n        ammonia\n       </a>\n       jumper between the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Port 3\n       </a>\n       (P3) and Port 6 (P6) truss segments. The spacewalkers furthermore installed a new light on the Crew Equipment Translation Aid (CETA) cart on the Starboard 3 (S3) truss segment, and a cover on the starboard\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#Solar_Alpha_Rotory_Joint" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Solar Alpha Rotary Joint\n       </a>\n       (SARJ). The installation of the wireless video system was completed during the third EVA. While the 6-hour-and-19-minute-long spacewalk was in progress, members of the STS-134 crew completed more equipment transfers between\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       and the ISS.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat09_52-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat09-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       crew members also prepared for the departure of\n       <a href="/wiki/Dmitri_Kondratyev" title="Dmitri Kondratyev">\n        Dmitri Kondratyev\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Nespoli" title="Paolo Nespoli">\n        Paolo Nespoli\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cady_Coleman" title="Cady Coleman">\n        Cady Coleman\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA1_Andrew_Feustel_5.jpg">\n class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n           <a class="image" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/STS_134_Feustel_EVA_1.jpg/214px-STS_134_Feustel_EVA_1.jpg 2x" width="107"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Feustel during EVA 1\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           EVA 1 choreographer Michael Fincke works on the aft flight deck of\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS134_Greg_Johnson.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848"
