class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           STS-134 pilot Greg Johnson\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="21_May_(Flight_Day_6)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="21_May_.28Flight_Day_6.29">\n        21 May (Flight Day 6)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: 21 May (Flight Day 6)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_tile_damage.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="356" data-file-width="430" height="182" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/STS-134_tile_damage.jpg/220px-STS-134_tile_damage.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/STS-134_tile_damage.jpg/330px-STS-134_tile_damage.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e7/STS-134_tile_damage.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_tile_damage.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         One of\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n          \'\n         </span>\n         s damaged\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermal_Protection_System" title="Thermal Protection System">\n          thermal protection tiles\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 6, the members of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s crew performed a focused inspection of an area of thermal protection tiles on the bottom of the orbiter. The tiles were damaged during launch, and detailed data provided by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) was needed to make sure the orbiter could re-enter Earth\'s atmosphere safely. The focused inspection started with the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       grappling the OBSS in the middle of the boom and handing it off to the shuttle\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        Canadarm\n       </a>\n       , which was controlled by pilot Greg Johnson and mission specialists Mike Fincke and Roberto Vittori. The inspection process took approximately two hours to complete, and resulted in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermal_Protection_System" title="Thermal Protection System">\n        Thermal Protection System\n       </a>\n       (TPS) being cleared for entry.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FI_53-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FI-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After the inspection was complete, Fincke joined Drew Feustel to get their spacesuits ready for the second spacewalk of the mission on flight day 7. The pair performed the standard overnight campout procedure to get ready for the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Activity" title="Extravehicular Activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       . Later in the crew day, the STS-134 crew assembled with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       crew in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kibo_(ISS_module)" title="Kibo (ISS module)">\n        Kibo\n       </a>\n       module. The joint crew spoke with\n       <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI" title="Pope Benedict XVI">\n        Pope Benedict XVI\n       </a>\n       , answering several questions asked by the Pope.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat11_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat11-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="22_May_(Flight_Day_7_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="22_May_.28Flight_Day_7_.E2.80.93_EVA_2.29">\n        22 May (Flight Day 7 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: 22 May (Flight Day 7 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1779" data-file-width="1974" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg/220px-Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg/330px-Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg/440px-Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Feustel_STS_134_EVA_2.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Feustel during EVA 2.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The second EVA of STS-134 was conducted on flight day 7 by Drew Feustel and Mike Fincke. The spacewalk, the sixth-longest in the history of spaceflight thus far,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       lasted 8 hours and 7 minutes, significantly longer than the planned 6 hours and 30 minutes. The excursion also marked the second-longest spacewalk conducted from the ISS. During the spacewalk, Fincke and Feustel hooked up a jumper to transfer 2.3\n       <a href="/wiki/Kilogram" title="Kilogram">\n        kg\n       </a>\n       (5\n       <a href="/wiki/Pound_(mass)" title="Pound (mass)">\n        lb\n       </a>\n       ) of\n       <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">\n        ammonia\n       </a>\n       to the Port 6 Photovoltaic Thermal Control System (PVTCS), lubricated the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#Solar_alpha_rotary_joint" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Solar Alpha Rotary Joint\n       </a>\n       (SARJ) and one of the "hands" on\n       <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n        Dextre\n       </a>\n       , and installed a stowage beam on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Starboard 1\n       </a>\n       (S1) truss. During the lubrication task on the Port SARJ, some of the bolts on one of the thermal blankets came free, and one was lost. Commander Mark Kelly documented the spacewalk with still and video cameras, while mission specialist Greg Chamitoff assisted Feustel and Fincke. The spacewalk was the seventh for Fincke and the fifth for Feustel. Fincke had conducted his previous six spacewalks in Russian\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orlan_spacesuit" title="Orlan spacesuit">\n        Orlan suits\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       While the EVA was conducted, the rest of the STS-134 crew completed more transfers between the ISS and\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat13_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat13-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flight day 7 also saw the ISS\' change of command ceremony. Russian cosmonaut\n       <a href="/wiki/Dmitri_Kondratyev" title="Dmitri Kondratyev">\n        Dmitri Kondratyev\n       </a>\n       , who had been the commander of\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       aboard the station, conducted a ceremonial change of command with cosmonaut\n       <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Borisenko" title="Andrei Borisenko">\n        Andrei Borisenko\n       </a>\n       , the commander of\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="23_May_(Flight_Day_8)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="23_May_.28Flight_Day_8.29">\n        23 May (Flight Day 8)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 23 May (Flight Day 8)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg/220px-STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg/330px-STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg/440px-STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS134_Mark_Kelly_in_the_middeck_of_Endeavour.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         STS-134 commander\n         <a href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly" title="Mark Kelly">\n          Mark Kelly\n         </a>\n         in the mid-deck of\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 8, the crew of STS-134 had some off duty time. Commander Mark Kelly and mission specialist Mike Fincke conducted an in-flight interview with 400 students from Mesa Verde Elementary School in\n       <a href="/wiki/Tucson,_Arizona" title="Tucson, Arizona">\n        Tucson, Arizona\n       </a>\n       . Later in the crew day, STS-134 mission specialist Roberto Vittori and\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_27" title="Expedition 27">\n        Expedition 27\n       </a>\n       flight engineer\n       <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Nespoli" title="Paolo Nespoli">\n        Paolo Nespoli\n       </a>\n       answered questions from Italian President\n       <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Napolitano" title="Giorgio Napolitano">\n        Giorgio Napolitano\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After the STS-134 crew went to bed, the Expedition 27 crew prepared for their departure. Expedition 27 commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Dmitri_Kondratyev" title="Dmitri Kondratyev">\n        Dmitri Kondratyev\n       </a>\n       and flight engineers Paolo Nespoli and\n       <a href="/wiki/Catherine_Coleman" title="Catherine Coleman">\n        Catherine Coleman\n       </a>\n       left the ISS aboard the\n       <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-20" title="Soyuz TMA-20">\n        Soyuz TMA-20\n       </a>\n       spacecraft at 21:35 UTC. The departure of the three Expedition 27 crew members marked the start of\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       , leaving the new expedition commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Borisenko" title="Andrei Borisenko">\n        Andrei Borisenko\n       </a>\n       and flight engineers\n       <a href="/wiki/Aleksandr_Samokutyayev" title="Aleksandr Samokutyayev">\n        Aleksandr Samokutyayev\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n        Ron Garan\n       </a>\n       aboard the station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat15_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat15-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Before re-entry, Soyuz TMA-20 performed a special fly-about of the ISS, taking numerous photographs of the station and of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a href="#cite_note-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Soyuz TMA-20 and the Expedition 27 crew landed safely in central\n       <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">\n        Kazakhstan\n       </a>\n       at 02:27 UTC on 24 May 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n        <a href="#cite_note-59">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_11.jpg/120px-ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_11.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_11.jpg/160px-ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_11.jpg 2x"          </a>\n           </i>\n           taken from\n           <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-20" title="Soyuz TMA-20">\n            Soyuz TMA-20\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px          </a>\n           </i>\n           taken from\n           <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-20" title="Soyuz TMA-20">\n            Soyuz TMA-20\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_30.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="4032" data-file-width="6048" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_30.jpg/120px-ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_30.jpg" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_30.jpg/240px-ISS_and_Endeavour_seen_from_the_Soyuz_TMA-20_spacecraft_30.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Photo of the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            ISS\n           </a>\n           and\n           <i>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           taken from\n           <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-20" title="Soyuz TMA-20">\n            Soyuz TMA-20\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="24_May_(Flight_Day_9)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="24_May_.28Flight_Day_9.29">\n        24 May (Flight Day 9)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: 24 May (Flight Day 9)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg/220px-Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg/330px-Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg/440px-Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mike_Fincke_and_Ron_Garan.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n          Mike Fincke\n         </a>\n         and\n         <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n          Expedition 28\n         </a>\n         crew member\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n          Ron Garan\n         </a>\n         pose for a photo.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 9, mission specialist Greg Chamitoff and pilot Greg Johnson conducted a series of interviews with media outlets around the United States, including\n       <a href="/wiki/KPIX-TV" title="KPIX-TV">\n        KPIX-TV\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/KGO-TV" title="KGO-TV">\n        KGO-TV\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/KFBK_(AM)" title="KFBK (AM)">\n        KFBK\n       </a>\n       . Later in the day, commander Mark Kelly and mission specialists Mike Fincke and Chamitoff conducted interviews with\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Daily_(News_Corporation)" title="The Daily (News Corporation)">\n        The Daily\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/KDKA_(AM)" title="KDKA (AM)">\n        KDKA\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pittsburgh_Tribune-Review" title="Pittsburgh Tribune-Review">\n        Pittsburgh Tribune-Review\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/KTRK-TV" title="KTRK-TV">\n        KTRK-TV\n       </a>\n       . Johnson and mission specialist Roberto Vittori also completed some more equipment transfers between the station and shuttle, and began to clean up and organize the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Permanent_Multipurpose_Module" title="Permanent Multipurpose Module">\n        Permanent Multipurpose Module\n       </a>\n       (PMM)\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       . The STS-134 crew furthermore completed some work on the\n       <a href="/wiki/ISS_ECLSS#Oxygen_generating_system" title="ISS ECLSS">\n        Oxygen Generator System\n       </a>\n       (OGS) and Carbon Dioxide Removal Assembly (CDRA). Drew Feustel, joined by Fincke and Chamitoff, spent most of the day preparing the tools for the following day\'s EVA. At the end of their day, the shuttle crew and\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       flight engineer\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n        Ron Garan\n       </a>\n       conducted an EVA procedures review in preparation for the third spacewalk on flight day 10.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat16_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat16-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="25_May_(Flight_Day_10_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="25_May_.28Flight_Day_10_.E2.80.93_EVA_3.29">\n        25 May (Flight Day 10 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: 25 May (Flight Day 10 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 10, the third spacewalk of the STS-134 mission was conducted. The spacewalk made use of a new spacewalk pre-breathe protocol, called In-Suit Light Exercise (ISLE), instead of the normal campout pre-breathe protocol. The new pre-breathe protocol had the astronauts breathe pure oxygen for 60 minutes in the airlock, which had its air pressure lowered to 10.2 Psi (703hPa). The astronauts then put their spacesuits on, performed light exercise and rested for an additional 50 minutes, breathing pure oxygen all the while. After astronauts\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n        Drew Feustel\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       exited the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quest_Airlock" title="Quest Airlock">\n        <i>\n         Quest\n        </i>\n        Airlock\n       </a>\n       , the pair began installing the Power Data Grapple Fixture (PDGF). The fixture itself and most of its components were installed, but the data cable associated with it was to be installed later. The spacewalking pair then moved on and routed some new power cables from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Unity_(ISS_module)" title="Unity (ISS module)">\n        <i>\n         Unity\n        </i>\n        module\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zarya_(ISS_module)" title="Zarya (ISS module)">\n        <i>\n         Zarya\n        </i>\n        module\n       </a>\n       on the Russian segment of the ISS, providing a redundant power supply to the Russian segment. Feustel and Fincke then moved on to finish up the installation of the wireless video system which Fuestel and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       had begun to install on EVA 1. The pair also took pictures of the\n       <i>\n        Zarya\n       </i>\n       module\'s thrusters and captured some\n       <a href="/wiki/Infrared" title="Infrared">\n        infrared\n       </a>\n       video of an experiment delivered on board the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Express_Logistics_Carrier" title="Express Logistics Carrier">\n        Express Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       (ELC) 3.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EVA3_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EVA3-61">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       documented the spacewalk from inside the station. While the EVA was going on, pilot\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       and mission specialist\n       <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Vittori" title="Roberto Vittori">\n        Roberto Vittori\n       </a>\n       assisted\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       flight engineer\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n        Ron Garan\n       </a>\n       in stowing new equipment and supplies on the ISS.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat19_62-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat19-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA3_Drew_Feustel_and_Michael_Fincke.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/STS-134_EVA3_Drew_Feustel_and_Michael_Fincke.jpg/240px-STS-134_EVA3_Drew_Feustel_and_Michael_Fincke.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Andrew_Feustel" title="Andrew Feustel">\n            Feustel\n           </a>\n           (right) and\n           <a href="/wiki/Michael_Fincke" title="Michael Fincke">\n            Fincke\n           </a>\n           work during EVA 3\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA_3_Andrew_Feustel.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80"    <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n            Drew Feustel\n           </a>\n           during EVA 3\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA3_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/STS-134_EVA3_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg/240px-STS-134_EVA3_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n            Mike Fincke\n           </a>\n           during EVA 3\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="26_May_(Flight_Day_11)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="26_May_.28Flight_Day_11.29">\n        26 May (Flight Day 11)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: 26 May (Flight Day 11)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg/220px-STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg/330px-STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg/440px-STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_in-flight_crew_portrait.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         In-flight STS-134 crew portrait in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Kibo_(ISS_module)" title="Kibo (ISS module)">\n          Kibo Lab\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 11, the crew of Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       conducted a late inspection of the orbiter\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermal_Protection_System" title="Thermal Protection System">\n        Thermal Protection System\n       </a>\n       . On most previous flights, this inspection was performed after the shuttle undocked from the ISS. However, in this case it was done early, because the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) was to be left on board the ISS after\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s departure.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd10_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd10-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The joint\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       /STS-134 crew held a news conference with reporters on the ground at NASA centers around the country and ISS partner agencies. Commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       also spoke to reporters from four\n       <a href="/wiki/Tucson,_Arizona" title="Tucson, Arizona">\n        Tucson\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">\n        Arizona\n       </a>\n       television stations. Later in the crew day, the joint crew held an EVA procedure review for the fourth and final spacewalk of STS-134. Astronauts\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       spent the night in the\n       <i>\n        Quest\n       </i>\n       Airlock with the air pressure reduced to 10.2 Psi, so as to avoid\n       <a href="/wiki/Decompression_sickness" title="Decompression sickness">\n        decompression sickness\n       </a>\n       during their spacewalk. The crew and flight controllers on the ground opted not to use the In-suit Light Exercise (ISLE) protocol that was tested during EVA 3 earlier in the mission, opting instead to go with the standard campout protocol, since it was discovered that ISLE used more carbon-dioxide scrubbing capability. They wanted to save this capability, since a CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       sensor in Chamitoff\'s suit had failed during EVA 1, cutting that spacewalk short.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat21_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat21-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="27_May_(Flight_Day_12_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_4)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="27_May_.28Flight_Day_12_.E2.80.93_EVA_4.29">\n        27 May (Flight Day 12 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 4)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: 27 May (Flight Day 12 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 4)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg/220px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg/330px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg/440px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_7.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n           Endeavour\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         docked at the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n          ISS\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The final spacewalk of the STS-134 mission, and the final spacewalk of the Space Shuttle program, was carried out on flight day 12. The EVA was conducted by\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Chamitoff" title="Gregory Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       , who began the EVA by installing the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Starboard 1\n       </a>\n       (S1) truss segment. After the OBSS was installed, Fincke and Chamitoff removed the End Effector Grapple Fixture (EFGF) and replaced it with a spare Power and Data Grapple Fixture (PDGF). The station\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       could not grapple the EFGF, so the PDGF was installed on the end. After that task was completed, Fincke and Chamitoff moved to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Express_Logistics_Carrier" title="Express Logistics Carrier">\n        Express Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       (ELC) 3, and released some torque on the bolts that were holding the spare arm for\n       <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n        Dextre\n       </a>\n       down against the ELC. The EVA saw the total cumulative time spent performing EVAs in support of the ISS pass the 1,000-hour mark. The three STS-134 spacewalkers spent a total time of 28 hours and 44 minutes outside the ISS on this mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eva4_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-eva4-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Commander Mark Kelly assisted with documenting the spacewalk by taking photos and video.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat23_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat23-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the meantime, the rest of the shuttle crew completed more equipment transfers from\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Johannes_Kepler_ATV" title="Johannes Kepler ATV">\n        Johannes Kepler ATV\n       </a>\n       to the ISS.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Working from the mid-deck of Endeavour, Andrew Feustel, who participated in the first three spacewalks of the mission, was the EVA 4 choreographer. Astronaut\n       <a href="/wiki/Steven_Swanson" title="Steven Swanson">\n        Steven Swanson\n       </a>\n       was the spacewalk CAPCOM from the station flight control room in Houston. During Flight Day 12, Mike Fincke achieved a milestone, becoming the U.S. astronaut with the most time in space, more than 377 days. He surpassed the time in space of astronaut\n       <a href="/wiki/Peggy_Whitson" title="Peggy Whitson">\n        Peggy Whitson\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/STS-134_EVA4_preparations_in_the_Quest_airlock.jpg/180px-STS-134_EVA4_preparations_in_the_Quest_airlock.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/STS-134_EVA4_Gregory_Chamitoff_4.jpg/240px-STS-134_EVA4_Gregory_Chamitoff_4.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Chamitoff" title="Gregory Chamitoff">\n            Gregory Chamitoff\n           </a>\n           during EVA 4\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg/120px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg/180px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg/240px-STS-134_EVA4_Michael_Fincke_1.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n            Fincke\n           </a>\n           works outside the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            ISS\n           </a>\n           during EVA 4\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:33px auto;">\n           <a class="image" class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Composite of images showing the view of the entire\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS" title="ISS">\n            ISS\n           </a>\n           as seen from\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ELC-3" title="ELC-3">\n            ELC-3\n           </a>\n           during EVA 4\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="28_May_(Flight_Day_13)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="28_May_.28Flight_Day_13.29">\n        28 May (Flight Day 13)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: 28 May (Flight Day 13)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 13 saw the members of the STS-134 crew complete several major tasks. Mission specialists Mike Fincke and Greg Chamitoff replaced an absorbent bed in the Carbon Dioxide Removal Assembly (CDRA). The beds have to be changed from time to time in order for the CDRA to remove\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carbon_Dioxide" title="Carbon Dioxide">\n        CO\n        <sub>\n         2\n        </sub>\n       </a>\n       . While the CDRA work was on-going, commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       and mission specialist\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n        Drew Feustel\n       </a>\n       re-sized two of the spacesuits that will be used by\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       flight engineers\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ron_Garan" title="Ron Garan">\n        Ron Garan\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fossum" title="Mike Fossum">\n        Mike Fossum\n       </a>\n       . The rest of the STS-134 crew completed more transfers between space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       and the International Space Station (ISS). Commander Mark Kelly, joined by pilot\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       and Ron Garan, spoke with students, teachers and others gathered at\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Arizona" title="University of Arizona">\n        University of Arizona\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Tucson,_Arizona" title="Tucson, Arizona">\n        Tucson\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">\n        Arizona\n       </a>\n       . Johnson also spoke with representatives of Gannet,\n       <a href="/wiki/KPRC-TV" title="KPRC-TV">\n        KPRC-TV\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Voice_of_America" title="Voice of America">\n        Voice of America\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat25_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat25-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="4256" data-file-width="2832" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg/80px-STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg/120px-STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg/160px-STS-134_Michael_Fincke_in_the_Kibo_laboratory.jpg 2x" width="80"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a href="/wiki/Michael_Fincke" title="Michael Fincke">\n            Fincke\n           </a>\n           performs CDRA maintenance work in the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kibo_laboratory" title="Kibo laboratory">\n            Kibo laboratory\n           </a>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg/120px-STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg/180px-STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg/240px-STS_134_Endeavour_Docked.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           , backdropped by a night time view of Earth and a starry sky\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="29_May_(Flight_Day_14)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="29_May_.28Flight_Day_14.29">\n        29 May (Flight Day 14)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: 29 May (Flight Day 14)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 14 was the final day for the STS-134 crew to complete activities on board the ISS. Pilot Greg Johnson joined Feustel early in the crew day and spoke with\n       <a href="/wiki/WJRT-TV" title="WJRT-TV">\n        WJRT-TV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Flint,_Michigan" title="Flint, Michigan">\n        Flint, Michigan\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WJBK-TV" title="WJBK-TV">\n        WJBK-TV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Detroit,_Michigan" title="Detroit, Michigan">\n        Detroit, Michigan\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WKYC-TV" title="WKYC-TV">\n        WKYC-TV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cleveland,_Ohio" title="Cleveland, Ohio">\n        Cleveland, Ohio\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WXMI-TV" title="WXMI-TV">\n        WXMI-TV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Rapids,_Michigan" title="Grand Rapids, Michigan">\n        Grand Rapids, Michigan\n       </a>\n       . The transfer of supplies and equipment was completed on flight day 14, with the transfer of 4 bags of water from the shuttle to the ISS. Mission specialist Mike Fincke completed the work on the Carbon Dioxide Removal Assembly (CDRA) that he and Greg Chamitoff had started the day before. Chamitoff was joined by Drew Feustel to finish stowing tools that had been used during the mission\'s four spacewalks. Space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s small\n       <a href="/wiki/Vernier_thruster" title="Vernier thruster">\n        vernier thrusters\n       </a>\n       were used to raise the ISS by about 960 metres (3,150\xc2\xa0ft).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat27_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat27-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The later part of the crew day saw the\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_28" title="Expedition 28">\n        Expedition 28\n       </a>\n       crew hold a farewell ceremony for the STS-134 crew. After the two crews said their farewells to one another, they got into procedures to close the hatches on the ISS and space shuttle. After the hatches were closed and secured, a series of leak checks were performed on both vehicles, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pressurized_Mating_Adapter#PMA-2" title="Pressurized Mating Adapter">\n        Pressurized Mating Adapter 2\n       </a>\n       (PMA 2) was depressurized. The hatch closures marked the end of joint operations which totaled 10 days, 23 hours and 45 minutes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-farewell_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-farewell-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="30_May_(Flight_Day_15_\xe2\x80\x93_Undocking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="30_May_.28Flight_Day_15_.E2.80.93_Undocking.29">\n        30 May (Flight Day 15 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: 30 May (Flight Day 15 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 15, Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       undocked from the International Space Station.\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       had been docked with the ISS for 11 days, 17 hours and 41 minutes. After the shuttle undocked, pilot\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       backed\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       out to a distance of 140\xc2\xa0m (450\xc2\xa0ft) to 200\xc2\xa0m (650\xc2\xa0ft). Once the shuttle was at the correct distance, Johnson flew a complete lap around the ISS. After the lap was complete, an initial separation burn was completed. After the burn was complete, commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       took over control of the shuttle. Kelly first moved the shuttle to a point 6,100\xc2\xa0m (20,000\xc2\xa0ft) behind and above the station, then to a point below the ISS. Kelly then guided\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       to a point 290\xc2\xa0m (950\xc2\xa0ft) below the ISS. This series of maneuvers was done to test the Sensor Test for Orion Relative Navigation Risk Mitigation (STORRM) sensors. For the rest of the day, the STS-134 crew conducted preparations for their reentry and landing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat29_70-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat29-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="31_May_(Flight_Day_16)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="31_May_.28Flight_Day_16.29">\n        31 May (Flight Day 16)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: 31 May (Flight Day 16)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 16, the members of space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s STS-134 crew continued preparations for the shuttle\'s landing on flight day 17. Commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mark_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Mark Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Mark Kelly\n       </a>\n       , pilot\n       <a href="/wiki/Gregory_H._Johnson" title="Gregory H. Johnson">\n        Greg Johnson\n       </a>\n       and mission specialist and flight engineer\n       <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Vittori" title="Roberto Vittori">\n        Roberto Vittori\n       </a>\n       performed a checkout of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       <span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">\n        \'\n       </span>\n       s Flight Control Systems (FCS). They began by starting\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Auxiliary_Power_Unit#Spacecraft" title="Auxiliary Power Unit">\n        Auxiliary Power Unit 1\n       </a>\n       (APU 1), so they could test the flight systems such as the ailerons and rudder. The APU was used to provide hydraulic pressure to power the flight control systems. The astronauts next moved on to a test of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reaction_Control_System" title="Reaction Control System">\n        Reaction Control System\n       </a>\n       (RCS) jets. This test saw Kelly, Johnson and Vittori fire each jet once. Meanwhile,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n        Drew Feustel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n        Mike Fincke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n        Greg Chamitoff\n       </a>\n       stowed items on the mid-deck for their return to Earth. Later in the crew day, they stowed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ku_band" title="Ku band">\n        K\n        <sub>\n         u\n        </sub>\n        band\n       </a>\n       antenna for re-entry. The crew also performed several experiments, including an eye exam and the Ram Burn Observation (RAMBO2) experiments, and conducted a deorbit briefing to go over the procedures for the landing. The entire crew furthermore participated in in-flight interviews with\n       <a href="/wiki/ABC_News" title="ABC News">\n        ABC News\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/CBS_News" title="CBS News">\n        CBS News\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">\n        CNN\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/NBC_News" title="NBC News">\n        NBC News\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fox_News_Radio" title="Fox News Radio">\n        Fox News Radio\n       </a>\n       , and sent a crew tribute to\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       down to the ground.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stat31_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stat31-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="1_June_(Flight_Day_17_\xe2\x80\x93_Re-entry_and_landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="1_June_.28Flight_Day_17_.E2.80.93_Re-entry_and_landing.29">\n        1 June (Flight Day 17 \xe2\x80\x93 Re-entry and landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: 1 June (Flight Day 17 \xe2\x80\x93 Re-entry and landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew was awakened by mission control at 5:57 PM\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">\n        Eastern Time\n       </a>\n       to begin flight day 17 to the song "Sunrise No. 1" by Stormy Mondays.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mcc32_72-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mcc32-72">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The payload bay doors on the shuttle were closed at 10:48\xc2\xa0p.m. EDT. At 1:29\xc2\xa0a.m. on 1 June, the de-orbit burn was initiated, finishing at 1:31\xc2\xa0a.m. The shuttle began\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atmospheric_reentry" title="Atmospheric reentry">\n        reentering\n       </a>\n       the atmosphere at approximately 2:03\xc2\xa0a.m. At 2:25\xc2\xa0a.m.,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       crossed the Florida coast. The shuttle landed safely in Florida at around 2:35\xc2\xa0a.m. EDT, completing its 25th and final mission into space.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn_13-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-edition.cnn.com_16-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-edition.cnn.com-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="1696" data-file-width="2549" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg/120px-STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg/180px-STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg/240px-STS-134_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour_makes_its_final_landing.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           touches down at the\n           <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n            Kennedy Space Center\n           </a>\n           on 1 June 2011.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_3.jpg/240px-STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_3.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           shortly after touchdown at\n           <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n            Kennedy Space Center\n           </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_7.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3000" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_7.jpg/120px-STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_7.jpg" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_7.jpg/240px-STS-134_landing_at_Kennedy_Space_Center_7.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n             Endeavour\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           after wheel stop at the\n           <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n            Kennedy Space Center\n           </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-134_crew_after_landing.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2639" data-file-width="3966" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/STS-134_crew_after_landing.jpg/120px-STS-134_crew_after_landing.jpg" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/STS-134_crew_after_landing.jpg/240px-STS-134_crew_after_landing.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           The crew pose for a photo on the runway after landing.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Spacewalks">\n        Spacewalks\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Spacewalks">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       There were four spacewalks (EVAs) completed by three astronauts during the flight.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-summary_73-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-summary-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The total time spent outside was 28 hours and 44 minutes. The EVAs are expected to be the final EVAs conducted by a shuttle crew.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="width: 5em;">\n         EVA\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Spacewalkers\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Start (\n         <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n          UTC\n         </a>\n         )\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         End (UTC)\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Duration\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Drew_Feustel" title="Drew Feustel">\n          Drew Feustel\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greg_Chamitoff" title="Greg Chamitoff">\n          Greg Chamitoff\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         20 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         07:10\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         20 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         13:29\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6 hours 19 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Feustel and Chamitoff retrieved the two\n         <a href="/wiki/Materials_International_Space_Station_Experiment" title="Materials International Space Station Experiment">\n          MISSE 7 experiments\n         </a>\n         and installed a new package of MISSE 8 experiments on\n         <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Express_Logistics_Carrier_2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Express Logistics Carrier 2 (page does not exist)">\n          ELC-2\n         </a>\n         , which was already on the station. They installed jumpers between segments on the left-side truss, or backbone, of the station, for\n         <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">\n          ammonia\n         </a>\n         refills, and vented\n         <a href="/wiki/Nitrogen" title="Nitrogen">\n          nitrogen\n         </a>\n         from an ammonia servicer. They also began to install an external wireless communication antenna on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Destiny_(ISS_module)" title="Destiny (ISS module)">\n          <i>\n           Destiny\n          </i>\n          laboratory\n         </a>\n         to provide wireless communication to the Express Logistics Carriers mounted on the station\'s truss, but the installation was cut short due to a bad\n         <a href="/wiki/Carbon_dioxide" title="Carbon dioxide">\n          CO\n          <sub>\n           2\n          </sub>\n         </a>\n         sensor in Chamitoff\'s suit.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Feustel\n         <br/>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Fincke" title="Mike Fincke">\n          Mike Fincke\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         22 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         06:05\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         22 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         14:12\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         8 hours 07 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Feustel and Fincke refilled the Port 6 (P5) radiators with ammonia. They completed venting the early ammonia system, and lubricated the port solar alpha rotary joint and parts of\n         <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n          Dextre\n         </a>\n         , a two-armed space station robot capable of handling delicate assembly tasks currently performed by spacewalkers. Fincke also installed grapple bars on the port radiators.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 3\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Feustel\n         <br/>\n         Fincke\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         25 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         05:43\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         25 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         12:37\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6 hours 54 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Feustel and Fincke installed a grapple fixture (a handle for the station\'s\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n          Canadarm2\n         </a>\n         to grab on to) on the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zarya_(ISS_module)" title="Zarya (ISS module)">\n          <i>\n           Zarya\n          </i>\n          module\n         </a>\n         , to support robotic operations based from the Russian segment. They also installed additional cables to provide backup power to the Russian portion of the space station. The pair finished installing the wireless video system that was left unfinished during EVA 1.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 4\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Fincke\n         <br/>\n         Chamitoff\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         27 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         04:15\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         27 May 2011\n         <br/>\n         11:39\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         7 hours 24 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Fincke and Chamitoff stowed the shuttle\'s 50-foot\n         <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n          Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n         </a>\n         (OBSS) on the right-side truss on a permanent stowage fixture. The pair then retrieved a grapple from the station\'s left-side truss and used it as a replacement for the grapple previously on the boom. They then released restraints from one of the spare arms for Dextre and replaced thermal insulation on one of the spare gas tanks for the\n         <a href="/wiki/Quest_Joint_Airlock" title="Quest Joint Airlock">\n          <i>\n           Quest\n          </i>\n          Airlock\n         </a>\n         . The spacewalk marked the completion of the\n         <a href="/wiki/US_Orbital_Segment" title="US Orbital Segment">\n          US Orbital Segment\n         </a>\n         of the ISS.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Launch_attempts">\n        Launch attempts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span   <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Wake-up_calls">\n        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-134&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       NASA began a tradition of playing music to astronauts during the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gemini_program" title="Gemini program">\n        Gemini program\n       </a>\n       , and first used music to wake up a flight crew during\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">\n        Apollo 15\n       </a>\n       . Each track is specially chosen, often by the astronauts\' families, and usually has a special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chronology_75-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-chronology-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wakeup_76-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wakeup-76">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       NASA opened the selection process to the public for the first time for\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-133" title="STS-133">\n        STS-133\n       </a>\n       , where the public was invited to vote on two songs used to wake up astronauts on previous missions to wake up the STS-133 crew. For STS-134, the public was invited to submit original songs, with two songs being selected to wake up the crew of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Flight Day\n
